***tussen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a> (398)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tusschen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twisschen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tusschen</i>, a shortening of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">intwiskan</i>, originally a prepositional phrase <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*in twiskan</i>. The latter word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twiskaz</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twiskijaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twofold, double</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dwís</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">twice, doubly; in two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***tutoyeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tutoyeren.html>tutoyeren</a> (32957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tutoyer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tutoyeren.html>tutoyeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to address someone casually by using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a></i> or the unemphatic <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a></i>, as opposed to formal <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">jijjouwen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">jijen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">jouen</span></li></ul>

***tutu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a> (42917)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cucu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bum, bottom</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, playful reduplication of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">cul</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:arse.html>arse</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tutus</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:ballet.html>ballet</a> skirt made of layered stiff but light netting.
<dl><dd><i>The <a href = vnd.unilang:ballet.html>ballet</a> dancer representing the swan wore a white <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/M%C4%81ori_language" class="extiw" title="w:Māori language">Maori</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tutu.html>tutu</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tutus</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of the genus <i>Coriaria</i> of shrubs and trees found in New Zealand.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">toot plant</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">tupakihi</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:twa.html>twa</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twai</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dwóh₁</i>.
</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twelef</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tweelf</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twalef</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twaelf</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*twelif</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*twalif</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twalif</i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zwölf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">tolve</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">twelve</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tolf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">tolv</i>.
</p>

***tweeling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a> (3366)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twiling</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twilling</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tweiling</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*twinling</i>, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twinilingaz</i>, with the first element from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*twinaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zwilling</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">twinling</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">tvilling</i>); or a more recent formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ling</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweelingen.html>tweelingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweelingetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pair of twins; <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> of people and other mammals.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">My brother and I are <b>twins</b>.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">My brother and I are a <b>twin [pair]</b>.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">less common, usually plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Each of two twin siblings.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tweeling.html>tweeling</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nooit.html>nooit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <b>twin</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> never alone.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A vegetal or object equivalent, e.g. an identical fruit pair</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaar.html>twijfelaar</a> (67022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">twivelaer</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelen.html>twijfelen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaar.html>twijfelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaars.html>twijfelaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twijfelaar.html>twijfelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A doubter, hesitater; one who doubts or hesitates.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> of a size that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in between those of a regular single size <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a> and a double <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>, typically with a breadth of 120 or 140 centimetres.</li></ol>

***twistgesprek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:twistgesprek.html>twistgesprek</a> (122492)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">twist</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gesprek.html>gesprek</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twistgesprek.html>twistgesprek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twistgesprekken.html>twistgesprekken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twistgesprek.html>twistgesprekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A dispute, an argument, a verbal controversy, in particular about political or religious topics. <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li></ol>

***tycoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tycoon.html>tycoon</a> (78774)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese language">Japanese</a></span> <i class="Jpan mention" lang="ja">大君</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-tr tr">taikun</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">great prince</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a title for the <span class="Latn" lang="en">shōgun</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">taipan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese"><a href = vnd.unilang:cantonese.html>Cantonese</a></a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="yue">大班</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">daai6 baan1</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tycoon.html>tycoon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">tycoons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wealthy and powerful business person.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>captain</a> of industry</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">magnate</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">mogul</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Chairman Yu <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tycoon.html>tycoon</a></b> who owns multiple <a href = vnd.unilang:hotel.html>hotel</a> chains.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1956</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delano_Ames" class="extiw" title="w:Delano Ames"><a href = vnd.unilang:delano.html>Delano</a> Ames</a>,  chapter 24, in  <cite>Crime out of Mind</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5915292W">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Dagobert <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> only one customer, an American who wore square, rimless glasses and a <a href = vnd.unilang:beige.html>beige</a> suit and looked like a Wall Street <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tycoon.html>tycoon</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">tycoonocracy</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">tycoonocrat</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">daimyō</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">taipan</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tycoon.html>tycoon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rijk.html>rijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deel.html>deel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> bedrijfstak in <a href = vnd.unilang:handen.html>handen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:indische.html>Indische</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tycoon.html>tycoon</a></b> Lakshmi Mittal <a href = vnd.unilang:kocht.html>kocht</a> in 2006 <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> staalbedrijf Arcelor <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daarmee.html>daarmee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eigenaar.html>eigenaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootste.html>grootste</a> staalproducent <a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***tyfoon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tyfoon.html>tyfoon</a> (40055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably ultimately of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sinitic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Sinitic languages">Sinitic</a></span> origin, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mandarin_Chinese" class="extiw" title="w:Mandarin Chinese">Mandarin</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="cmn">大风</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cmn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dàfēng</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cantonese" class="extiw" title="w:Cantonese"><a href = vnd.unilang:cantonese.html>Cantonese</a></a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="yue">大風</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yue-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">daai<sup>6</sup> fung<sup>1</sup></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">big wind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طُوفَان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭūfān</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hindi" class="extiw" title="w:Hindi">Hindi</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="hi">तूफ़ान</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="hi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tūfān</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">توفان</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tufân</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Τυφῶν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Tuphôn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Typhon, father of the <a href = vnd.unilang:winds.html>winds</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unrelated but <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> secondarily contaminated the word:
given the location of typhoons as a Pacific Ocean phenomenon, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more likely it began east and moved west.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tyfoon.html>tyfoon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tyfoons.html>tyfoons</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tyfoon.html>tyfoontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">typhoon</span></li>
<li>train horn</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tyfoon.html>tyfoon</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:meteorologie.html>meteorologie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hevige.html>hevige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wervelstorm.html>wervelstorm</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Chinese <a href = vnd.unilang:zee.html>Zee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stille.html>Stille</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oceaan.html>Oceaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontstaat.html>ontstaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tropische.html>tropische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:depressie.html>depressie</a>

***tyfus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tyfus.html>tyfus</a> (11711)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">typhus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τῦφος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tûphos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fever, stupor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> term used for typhus and typhoid fever</li></ol>

***tyr.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tyr.html>tyr</a> (22072)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Danish language">Old Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmq-oda">thiur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">þjórr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*þeuraz</i>. The West Germanic languages have a form with <i>s-</i>: <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">steer</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stier.html>stier</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:stier.html>Stier</a></i>. These Germanic <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> seem to be related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">taurus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ταῦρος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taûros</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bull</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which may go back to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)táwros</i> (<i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)téh₂wros</i>). However, the vocalism of the Germanic <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> problematic. Furthermore, the similarity with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Semitic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Semitic language">Proto-Semitic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sem-pro">*ṯawr-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bull, ox</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> suggests that the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a wanderword.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="da"><a href = vnd.unilang:tyr.html>tyr</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span> (<i>singular definite</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-da def | s-form-of" lang="da">tyren</b>, <i>plural indefinite</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-da indef | p-form-of" lang="da">tyre</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bull <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">uncastrated adult male of cattle</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>Taurean <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">someone with the Taurus star sign</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="da">tyre</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="da">Tyren</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> (28)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally the accusative/dative form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">iu</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*iwwiz</i>, West Germanic variant of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*izwiz</i>, dative/accusative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*jūz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*yū́</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jou.html>jou</a></i>.
</p><p>The use as a nominative stems from an original possessive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:uwe.html>uwe</a> edelheid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">your nobility, your gentility</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> shortened to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a> E.</i> and finally to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:jo.html>jo</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:jo.html>jo</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:ju.html>ju</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">you</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">euch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_7">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The capitalization of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> (as in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a></i> or <i><a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>Uw</a></i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now considered old-fashioned, and no longer compulsory. In religious contexts, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still often capitalized, when addressing <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>.</li>
<li><i>See usage notes at</i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.</li></ul>

***ugh.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ugh.html>ugh</a> (36550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ugh.html>ugh</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Used to express repugnance, disgust, or annoyance.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ugh.html>Ugh</a></b>! The bread in the <a href = vnd.unilang:pantry.html>pantry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> moldy.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1855</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Browning" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Robert Browning">Robert Browning</a>, <a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Childe_Roland_to_the_Dark_Tower_Came" class="extiw" title="s:Childe Roland to the Dark Tower Came">“Childe Roland to the Dark Tower Came”</a>, XXI:
<dl><dd>[...] It may have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> a water-rat I speared, / But, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ugh.html>ugh</a></b>! it sounded like a <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a>'s shriek.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>See Thesaurus:<a href = vnd.unilang:yuck.html>yuck</a></li></ul>
</body>
